---
title: "Video fanart, coverart and banners gone after daily jamu cron"
date: 2010-01-07
forum: Mythbuntu
---

### Post by williammanda on 2010-01-07
My fanart, coverart and banners disappear each day after the jamu cron is run. I go in and reset the metadata for all the videos each day and then I noticed that the metadata was still there but the path for each one incorrect. The path should be /var/lib/mythtv/coverart/filename.jpg but it is just filename.jpg. Any ideas? Here's the jamu log file:

### Post by larsolav on 2010-01-07
Ha! Same happened to me! I am not using storage groups. I lost all the art for the ISO files I have, but curiously, not for DVDs ripped to VIDEO_TS format. Sorry for posting a "me to", but just didn't want you to feel lonely...

---

### Post by williammanda on 2010-01-19
After experimenting with another format for videos and understanding SG better I was able to get SG and artwork working properly. I had a talk with a user on mythtv-users and they explained that to use artwork with videos you needed to also use SG. It's all or none. I was using nfs mounts for videos (no SG) and artwork with SG. This was the reason for the issue I had. Once I switched to all SG everything seems to be working correctly. Also I changed the video format to mkv due to iso & vob formats do not work. This format works with SG, See this other post for details.

[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1384481]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1384481")

---
